# DO NOT CHANGE THE POSITIONS OF cut_down_to_size_no_infamy, cut_down_to_size_no_add_wargoal, or status_quo - IT BREAKS WAR INTERVENTION
#
# INSTRUCTIONS:
# -------------
# constructing_cb - default to yes. if "no", cant be picked for generation or as add_wargoal if no CB already
# is_triggered_only - Triggered from within the code or by event effects. DO NOT REMOVE THE STOCK ONES.
# mutual - The CB effects will also be used by the defender in peace treaties
# months - The number of months this CB will be valid. Only works for triggered CBs.
# prerequisites - A condition that automatically activates a CB. Does not work for triggered CBs. 'THIS' scope is the target country.
# badboy_factor - Multiplied with any badboy increase normally associated with a peace option.
# prestige_factor - Multiplied with any prestige increase normally associated with a peace option.
# peace_cost_factor - Multiplied with the cost of the peace options in the peace treaty
# po_xxx - Peace options. If toggled on, badboy_factor and prestige_factor are multiplied with any associated base changes to these (see defines.txt.)
# allowed_states - If 'po_demand_states' is on, badboy_factor applies to these provinces. 'THIS' scope is us.
# on_add - effect triggered when war goal added (triggering country's scope)
# construction_speed - base modifier for how long creating this CB will take. default is 1. 1.2 means 20% faster
# great_war_obligatory - cb is always added to the peace offer/demand in great wars.
# po_remove_cores - may be used only with: po_transfer_provinces, po_demand_state, po_annex
# crisis - can be offered as a wargoal in a crisis
#
# The peace options are:
#po_annex
#po_demand_state
#po_add_to_sphere
#po_disarmament
#po_reparations
#po_transfer_provinces
#po_remove_prestige
#po_make_puppet
#po_release_puppet
#po_status_quo
#po_install_communist_gov_type
#po_uninstall_communist_gov_type
#po_remove_cores
#po_colony

# NOTE: The order in which the peace options are listed is the order in which the AI will normally prioritize them in peace treaties

# TRIGGERED - Triggered from within the code or by event effects
# --------------------------------------------------------------

# A note on naval requirements for overseas targets: `num_of_ports` has a curious behaviour where
# paths from the capital to coastal provinces are computed and the final result only accounts for
# those that are reachable. (This may only apply for inland capitals.)
#
# In particular hostile sieges (including those from rebels) block those computed paths, but not
# much else does. This bears repeating: a country may be fully occupied and/or covered in *roaming*
# armies, and this won't affect what `num_of_ports` reports. However if a single rebel brigade
# starts a 100-year siege on the capital in a country that is otherwise free of troubles, suddenly
# the whole country counts as being landlocked. (This singular behaviour also includes the fact that
# occupied ports seem to be accounted for, though paths to the owner's capital are never computed
# for them.)
#
# To sidestep these quirks and spare players the frustration of spuriously invalidated CBs, a
# different requirement is used instead: `any_owned_province = { port = yes }`.

# Order that CBs are executed in a peace treaty

# Great War CB's
dismantle_cb = {
    sprite_index = 20
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

	constructing_cb = no
	always = yes
    #construction_speed = 0.25

    badboy_factor = 2
    prestige_factor = 10
    peace_cost_factor = 35
    penalty_factor = 3

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 3
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 108

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    can_use = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					is_greater_power = yes
					is_secondary_power = yes
					colonial_nation = yes
					any_owned_province = { is_overseas = yes }
				}
				is_disarmed = no
				is_vassal = no
				NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = target_of_dismantlement }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0.99 } }
				OR = {
					NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -100 } }
					war_with = THIS
				}
				THIS = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0.99 } }
					is_greater_power = yes
					is_disarmed = no
					mass_politics = 1
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = in_great_war
						has_country_modifier = no_more_war
						has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				THIS = {
					ai = no
					has_country_flag = literally_cheating
				}
			}
		}
    }

    po_disarmament = yes
    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = WAR_DISMANTLE_NAME

    on_add = {
        FROM = {
            set_country_flag = target_of_dismantlement
        }
		THIS = {
			country_event = 4778743
		}
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = pro_military
            to = jingoism
            value = 0.10
        }
        #country_event = 96000
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
		set_country_flag = Major_Defeated
		THIS = { set_country_flag = conference_sanity_check }
		CLN = { country_event = 4778746 }
    }
}

# Acquire Core State
acquire_core_state = {
    sprite_index = 5
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.7
    penalty_factor = 1
    always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            war_with = THIS
            any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS }
        }
        number_of_states = 1 # annex if you want their last state
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
		is_substate = no
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1834 }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier } }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
        #NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_CORE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        country_event = 2650    # Territorial Loss event
    }
}

# Acquire All Core States
acquire_all_cores = {
    sprite_index = 5
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    constructing_cb = no
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.7
    penalty_factor = 1
    always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
        civilized = yes
        number_of_states = 2 # annex if you want their last state
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                AND = {
                    war_policy = pacifism
                    war = no
                }
            }
        }
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1834 }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        any_owned_province = { NOT = { is_core = THIS } }
    }

    allowed_countries = {
        FROM = { tag = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
        #NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            AND = {
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
        }
    }

    all_allowed_states = yes
    po_transfer_provinces = yes

    war_name = WAR_ALL_CORES_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        country_event = 2650    # Territorial Loss event
    }
}

restore_austrian_empire = {
    sprite_index = 21
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.7
    penalty_factor = 1
    always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		any_owned_province = {
			any_neighbor_province = {
				owner = { tag = AUS }
			}
		}
        THIS = {
            tag = AUS
            OR = {
                war_policy = jingoism
                war_policy = pro_military
                war_with = THIS
            }
            OR = {
                is_greater_power = yes
                is_secondary_power = yes
            }
            OR = {
                government = absolute_empire
                government = semi_constitutional_empire
                government = constitutional_empire
                government = fascist_dictatorship
            }
        }
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                is_core = VEN
                is_core = SLO
                is_core = SLV
                is_core = BOH
                is_core = HUN
                is_core = GLM
                region = AUS_771
                region = AUS_780
                region = AUS_777
                region = AUS_654
                region = AUS_647
                region = AUS_652
                region = AUS_657
            }
			NOT = { province_id = 742 } #Neum
			NOT = { province_id = 741 } #Neum
			NOT = { province_id = 743 } #Neum
			NOT = { province_id = 3277 } #Hultschin/Hlucin/Hlucin
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { tag = ITA }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = accepts_italy } }
        }
        NOT = {
			tag = HUN
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1834 }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
            }
			has_global_flag = outside_cores_removed
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        NOT = { in_sphere = THIS }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = ai_demand_sigmaringen }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = outside_cores_removed }
		NOT = {
			OR = { tag = PLC tag = PLR tag = POL }
			has_global_flag = poland_happy_ending
		}
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                is_core = VEN
                is_core = SLO
                is_core = SLV
                is_core = BOH
                is_core = HUN
                is_core = GLM
                region = AUS_702
                region = AUS_771
                region = AUS_780
                region = AUS_777
                region = AUS_654
				region = AUS_647
                region = AUS_652
                region = AUS_657
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_AUSTRIAN_EMPIRE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                is_core = KRA
                is_core = GLM
            }
            remove_core = KRA
        }
    }

}

restore_america = {
    sprite_index = 21
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0
    peace_cost_factor = 0.7
    penalty_factor = 1
    always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            OR = {
                primary_culture = yankee
                primary_culture = dixie
            }
            NOT = { tag = USA }
        }
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                is_core = USA
                is_core = CSA
                is_core = FSA
            }
        }
        war_policy = jingoism
		any_owned_province = {
			any_neighbor_province = {

add_to_sphere = {
    sprite_index = 3
    is_triggered_only = yes

    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 35
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
        OR = {
			part_of_sphere = no
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        is_greater_power = no
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    ai = yes
                    nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
                }
                culture_has_union_tag = yes
                is_culture_group = THIS
                NOT = { is_cultural_union = THIS }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { total_pops = 11000000 }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
    }

    po_add_to_sphere = yes

    war_name = WAR_ADD_SPHERE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    has_country_flag = surrender_sudan_on_lose
                }
            }
            owner = {
                clr_country_flag = surrender_sudan_on_lose
                any_owned = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            is_core = SUD
                            is_core = ETH
                        }
                    }
                    secede_province = THIS
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 15
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 12

    always = yes

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        is_greater_power = yes
        culture_has_union_tag = yes
        is_culture_group = THIS
        cultural_union = { exists = no }
        NOT = { has_cultural_sphere = yes }
        THIS = {
            is_greater_power = yes
            nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
            NOT = { tag = KUK }
            NOT = { tag = UBD }
            NOT = { tag = DNB }
            ai = yes
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { tag = KUK }
        NOT = { tag = UBD }
        NOT = { tag = DNB }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes

    tws_battle_factor = 2.0 # battle score twice that of oppenent

    war_name = UNIFICATION_HUMILIATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        prestige_factor = -0.2
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Sphere of Influence Gain

    sprite_index = 3

    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 50
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    always = yes

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        culture_has_union_tag = yes
        is_culture_group = THIS
        OR = {
			part_of_sphere = no
            war_with = THIS
        }
        is_greater_power = no
        cultural_union = { exists = no }
        THIS = {
            is_greater_power = yes
            nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
            NOT = { tag = KUK }
            NOT = { tag = UBD }
            NOT = { tag = DNB }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war }
            ai = yes
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }

    po_add_to_sphere = yes

            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

#Take from Sphere CB's
take_from_sphere = {
    sprite_index = 4
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 2
    prestige_factor = 3
    peace_cost_factor = 20
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
        is_greater_power = yes
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        is_sphere_leader_of = FROM
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = FROM }
        OR = {
            FROM = { is_vassal = no }
            THIS = { is_our_vassal = FROM }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = {
				OR = {
					capital_scope = { continent = africa }
					capital_scope = { continent = west_africa }
					capital_scope = { continent = central_africa }
					capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
					capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }
				}
                civilized = no
            }
            FROM = { is_secondary_power = yes }
            FROM = { any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			} }
            FROM = { is_culture_group = THIS }
            THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
                }
                FROM = {
                    culture_has_union_tag = yes
                    is_culture_group = THIS
                    cultural_union = { exists = no }
                    sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    po_add_to_sphere = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_SPHERE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

#Free Peoples CB's
free_peoples = {
    sprite_index = 9
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            war_with = THIS
            any_neighbor_country = { OR = { vassal_of = THIS substate_of = THIS in_sphere = THIS } }
        }
        number_of_states = 2
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        FROM = {
            OR = {
                NOT = { has_country_flag = unreleasable_country }
                exists = yes
            }
        }
        NOT = {
            FROM = { war_with = THIS }
            FROM = { is_substate = yes }
        }
        NOT = {
            tag = FROM
            FROM = { tag = THIS }
            FROM = { tag = MTC }
            FROM = { tag = ETH }
            FROM = { tag = UKR }
            FROM = { tag = HND }
            FROM = { tag = PLC }
			FROM = { tag = PLR }
			FROM = { has_country_flag = i_am_phc }
			FROM = { has_country_flag = i_am_wsf }
            FROM = { tag = TPG }
            FROM = { tag = POL }
            FROM = { tag = QNG }
            FROM = { tag = CHI }
            FROM = { tag = CSA }
            FROM = { tag = USA }
            FROM = { tag = KAM }
            FROM = { tag = KAZ }
            FROM = { tag = BDK }
            FROM = { tag = SIB }
            FROM = { tag = YAK }
            FROM = { tag = ALT }
            FROM = { tag = URA }
            FROM = { tag = MCK }
            FROM = { tag = XIN }
            this_culture_union = FROM
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = ETH }
                ETH = { exists = no }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = BOL }
                exists = PBC
            }
        }
        FROM = {
            OR = {
                exists = yes
                is_cultural_union = no
                involved_in_crisis = yes
            }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { civilized = yes }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            FROM = { NOT = { any_core = { owned_by = THIS } } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { exists = no }
            FROM = { alliance_with = THIS }
            FROM = { in_sphere = THIS }
            FROM = { relation = { who = THIS value = 100 } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            AND = {
                tag = EGY
                THIS = { has_country_flag = oriental_crisis_support_OE }
                FROM = { tag = TUR }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        any_owned_province = {
            is_core = FROM
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            FROM = { exists = yes }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            FROM = {
                exists = no
                NOT = {
                    tag = CAT
                    tag = BSQ
                    tag = UKR
                    tag = KDS
                    tag = IRQ
                    tag = GEO
                }
            }
            AND = {
                owns = 498
                FROM = { tag = CAT }
            }
            AND = {
                owns = 492
                FROM = { tag = BSQ }
            }
            AND = {
                owns = 958
                FROM = { tag = UKR }
            }
            AND = {
                owns = 893
                FROM = { tag = KDS }
            }
            AND = {
                owns = 926
                FROM = { tag = IRQ }
            }
            AND = {
                owns = 1095
                FROM = { tag = GEO }
            }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state
    allowed_states = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }

                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {

                        controlled_by = THIS

            AND = {
                FROM = { exists = no }
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                FROM = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    OR = {
                        any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS }
                        any_neighbor_province = {
                            owner = {
                                OR = {
                                    in_sphere = THIS
                                    alliance_with = THIS
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        controlled_by = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { exists = no }
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    continent = europe
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {

                any_owned_province = {

                        continent = north_america
                        continent = south_america

                    is_core = FROM
                }

                any_owned_province = {
                    OR = {
                        continent = north_america
                        continent = south_america
                    }
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {

                THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = asia } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    continent = asia
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { exists = no }
                THIS = { civilized = yes }

                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            FROM = { exists = yes }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            FROM = {
                exists = no
                NOT = {
                    tag = POL

                    tag = BOH
                    tag = ALB
                    tag = LIT
                    tag = BOS
                    tag = CRO
                    tag = BUL
                    tag = SIE
                    tag = LUX
                }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    OR = {
                        region = PRU_701
                        region = RUS_706
                        region = RUS_715
                        region = AUS_702
                    }
                }
                FROM = { tag = POL }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    OR = {
                        region = AUS_641
                        region = AUS_623
                    }
                }
                FROM = { tag = HUN }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { region = AUS_771 }
                FROM = { tag = CRO }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { region = TUR_810 }
                FROM = { tag = BUL }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { region = AUS_625 }
                FROM = { tag = BOH }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { region = TUR_853 }
                FROM = { tag = ALB }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { region = TUR_788 }
                FROM = { tag = BOS }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { region = RUS_360 }
                FROM = { tag = LIT }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { region = AUS_657 }
                FROM = { tag = SIE }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { province_id = 397 }
                FROM = { tag = LUX }
            }
        }
    }

    po_transfer_provinces = yes

    war_name = WAR_FREE_NAME

    on_add = {
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { ai = no } }
            owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = disable_conquest_cb duration = -1 } }
        }
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25

		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Liberate country
liberate_country = {
    sprite_index = 15
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1


    can_use = {
        number_of_states = 2
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
            has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam
            has_global_flag = italy_fights_turk
            has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty
            has_global_flag = persia_treaty
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
            has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam
            has_global_flag = italy_fights_turk
            has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty
            has_global_flag = persia_treaty
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        #Prevent the CB being used on substates and on countries you are at war with
        NOT = {
            FROM = { war_with = THIS }
            FROM = { is_substate = yes }
        }

        FROM = {
            OR = {
                NOT = { has_country_flag = unreleasable_country }
                exists = yes
            }
        }

        OR = {
            is_releasable_vassal = FROM
            FROM = { exists = yes }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam }
            THIS = { has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty }
            THIS = { has_global_flag = persia_treaty }
            THIS = { ai = no }
            FROM = { NOT = { any_core = { is_core = THIS } } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        NOT = {
            tag = FROM
            FROM = { tag = THIS }
            FROM = { tag = MTC }
            this_culture_union = FROM
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = ETH }
                NOT = { exists = ETH }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = BOL }
                exists = PBC
            }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                OR = {
                    THIS = { ai = no }
                    THIS = { has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty }
                    THIS = { has_global_flag = persia_treaty }
                    has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty
                    has_global_flag = persia_treaty
                    THIS = { has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam }
                    has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam
                }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { exists = yes }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                involved_in_crisis = yes
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { exists = no }
                THIS = { civilized = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    OR = {
                        any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS }
                        controlled_by = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { exists = no }
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                FROM = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    OR = {
                        any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS }
                        any_neighbor_province = {
                            owner = {
                                OR = {
                                    in_sphere = THIS
                                    alliance_with = THIS
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        controlled_by = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {

                    continent = europe

        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            FROM = { civilized = yes }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty }
            has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty
            THIS = { has_global_flag = persia_treaty }
            has_global_flag = persia_treaty
            THIS = { has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam }
            has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { exists = no }
            FROM = { alliance_with = THIS }
            FROM = { in_sphere = THIS }
            FROM = { relation = { who = THIS value = 100 } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            AND = {
                tag = EGY
                THIS = { has_country_flag = oriental_crisis_support_OE }
                FROM = { tag = TUR }
            }
            tag = AFG
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty }
            has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty
            THIS = { has_global_flag = persia_treaty }
            has_global_flag = persia_treaty
            THIS = { has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam }
            has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state
    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
    }
    all_allowed_states = yes
    po_transfer_provinces = yes
    po_release_puppet = yes

    war_name = WAR_LIBERATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { ai = no } }
            owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = disable_conquest_cb duration = -1 } }
        }
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        THIS = { remove_country_modifier = disable_conquest_cb }
        country_event = 2651    # Territorial Loss event
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { tag = TUR owns = 846 has_global_flag = italy_fights_turk war_with = ITA } }
            ITA = { country_event = 900009 }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { tag = TUR NOT = { owns = 846 } has_global_flag = italy_fights_turk war_with = ITA } }
            ITA = { country_event = 900109 }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { tag = RUS has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty } }
            RUS = { clr_global_flag = wakhan_treaty }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { tag = RUS has_global_flag = persia_treaty } }
            RUS = { clr_global_flag = persia_treaty }
        }
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

					USA = { has_country_flag = maine_incident }
                }
            }
            OR = {
                exists = yes
                is_cultural_union = no
            }

    # THIS - us

    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 1
    prestige_factor = 5
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 0

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    always = yes

    can_use = {
        in_default = THIS
        THIS = {
            is_greater_power = yes
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }
        OR = {
            has_country_modifier = in_bankrupcy
            has_country_modifier = generalised_debt_default
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 50 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    po_gunboat = yes

    war_name = WAR_GUNBOAT_NAME
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Cut Down to size
cut_down_to_size = {
    sprite_index = 8
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 1.3
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 25
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    po_disarmament = yes
    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = CUT_DOWN_TO_SIZE_WAR_NAME

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            war_with = THIS
            any_neighbor_country = { OR = { vassal_of = THIS substate_of = THIS in_sphere = THIS } }
        }
        is_disarmed = no
        THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier } }
        THIS = { civilized = yes }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
		NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
    }

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    civilized = no
                    OR = {
                        owns = 1498 #Macao
                        owns = 1538 #Shanghai
						owns = 3364 #Sanmen
                        owns = 1496 #Hong Kong
                        owns = 1566    #Qingdao
                        owns = 1481 #Lushun - Port Arthur
                        owns = 1569 #Weihaiwei
                        owns = 1606 #Jiaxing
                        owns = 2681 #Taibei
                        owns = 2562 #Tainan
                        owns = 1499 #Hainan
                        owns = 2632 #Kwangchowan
                        #owns = 1540 #Nantong
                        owns = 1071 #Qeshm
                        owns = 1695 #Ifni
						owns = 3682 #Tarfaya
						owns = 3841 #Juzur Khuriya Muriya
						owns = 3820 #Barbara
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    civilized = yes
                    NOT = { is_culture_group = east_asian }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
            owner = {
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = { has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty_two }
							has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = negotiating_unequal_treaty_two
							duration = 30
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty
								has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty_two
							}
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = negotiating_unequal_treaty
							duration = 30
						}
					}
				}
			}
			THIS = {
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							has_country_modifier = negotiating_treaty
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = { name = negotiating_treaty_two duration = 30 }
					}
				}
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = { has_country_modifier = negotiating_treaty }
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = { name = negotiating_treaty duration = 30 }
					}
				}
			}
        }
        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { civilized = no has_country_modifier = uncivilized_isolationism } }
            owner = { remove_country_modifier = uncivilized_isolationism }
        }
        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { civilized = no NOT = { has_country_modifier = western_influences } } }
            owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = western_influences duration = -1 } }
        }
        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { civilized = no NOT = { capital_scope = { has_country_modifier = legation_quarter } } } }
            owner = { capital_scope = { add_province_modifier = { name = legation_quarter duration = -1 } } }
        }
        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = holding_tangiers owns = 1686 } }
            owner = { 1686 = { secede_province = THIS } clr_country_flag = holding_tangiers }
            THIS = { 1686 = { secede_province = MOR } }
        }
        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = refused_to_cede_congo } }
            owner = { any_owned = { limit = { is_core = CNG } secede_province = THIS } clr_country_flag = refused_to_cede_congo }
            THIS = { any_owned = { limit = { is_core = CNG } secede_province = CNG } }
        }

        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = { has_country_flag = lied_about_congo }
                THIS = { has_country_flag = claiming_congo }
            }
            owner = {
                any_country = { clr_country_flag = claiming_congo }
                clr_country_flag = lied_about_congo
                any_owned = {
                    limit = { is_core = CNG }
                    secede_province = THIS
                }
            }
        }
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }

    }
}

great_game_cb = {
    sprite_index = 22
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0.5
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.35
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    always = yes
    po_make_puppet = yes
    po_add_to_sphere = yes

    tws_battle_factor = 1.0

    war_name = WAR_PUPPET_NAME

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            is_greater_power = yes
            OR = {
                tag = ENG
                tag = RUS
            }
            OR = {
                government = absolute_monarchy
                government = prussian_constitutionalism
                government = hms_government
                government = absolute_empire
                government = semi_constitutional_empire
                government = constitutional_empire
            }
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = no_more_great_game
                has_country_modifier = punitive_effects
                badboy = 0.85
            }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS }
        }
        is_vassal = no
        civilized = no
        war = no
        OR = {
            AND = { tag = KOK THIS = { tag = RUS } }
            AND = { tag = KHI THIS = { tag = RUS } }
            AND = { tag = BUK THIS = { tag = RUS } }
            AND = { tag = BDK THIS = { tag = RUS } }
            AND = {
                tag = PNJ
                has_global_flag = 1_anglo_sikh_war
            }
            AND = {
                tag = BHU
                has_country_flag = anglo_bhutan_war
            }
            AND = {
                tag = AFG
                THIS = { tag = RUS }
                KOK = {
                    all_core = {
                        OR = {
                            owned_by = THIS
                            owner = {
                                vassal_of = THIS
                                war = no
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                KHI = {
                    all_core = {
                        OR = {
                            owned_by = THIS
                            owner = {
                                vassal_of = THIS
                                war = no
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                BUK = {
                    all_core = {
                        OR = {
                            owned_by = THIS
                            owner = {
                                vassal_of = THIS
                                war = no
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                OR = {
                    BDK = { OR = { all_core = { OR = { owned_by = THIS owner = { vassal_of = THIS war = no } } } vassal_of = THIS } }
                    1208 = { OR = { owned_by = THIS owner = { vassal_of = THIS war = no } } }
                }
            }
        }
		OR = {
			NOT = { tag = AFG }
			AND = {
				tag = AFG
				THIS = { NOT = { has_global_flag = afghanistan_is_neutral } }
			}
		}
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        NOT = {
            has_global_flag = british_dismantled
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            truce_with = THIS
            in_sphere = THIS
        }
    }

    on_add = {
        badboy = 3.5

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						tag = MAK
						tag = KAL
						tag = LAS
					}
				}
			}
			THIS = { badboy = -2.5 }
		}

        random_country = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    tag = RUS
                    tag = ENG
                }
                NOT = { tag = THIS }
            }
            relation = { who = THIS value = -50 }
        }
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        country_event = 19370
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}
