# Humiliate
humiliate = {
    sprite_index = 11
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 15
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
            }
			OR = {
				war_with = THIS
				THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
			}
			OR = {
				THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
				THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
				war_with = THIS
				NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
				THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
			OR = {
				prestige = 10
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
			OR = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = { tag = THIS }
					}
				}
				THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
			}
			#AI GP's will not invoke Humiliate when they have Unification Humiliate available
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					culture_has_union_tag = yes
					is_culture_group = THIS
					is_greater_power = yes
					cultural_union = { exists = no }
					NOT = { has_cultural_sphere = yes }
					THIS = {
						ai = yes
						is_greater_power = yes
						nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = recently_lost_war }
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                is_greater_power = no
            }
        }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes

    tws_battle_factor = 2.0

    war_name = WAR_HUMILIATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        prestige_factor = -0.2
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

#Acquire colonial state CB's
place_in_the_sun = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 1.1
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = yes }
        THIS = {
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
            OR = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        NOT = { owned_by = THIS }
                        is_colonial = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        #AI Pacifist will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = pacifism } }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI Anti Military will not use this commonly
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI after the Berlin Conference will need to hate each other guts to use this
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_global_flag = berlin_conference }
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -100 } }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = yes }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = {
                    OR = {
                        any_core = { exists = yes }
                        any_core = { exists = no }
                    }
                }
            }
            any_owned_province = {
                any_core = { civilized = no }
            }
            any_owned_province = { continent = africa }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			#Player in MP can take anything they want from other players
			AND = {
				owner = { ai = no }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}

            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}

            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }

            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        is_greater_power = yes
                        is_secondary_power = yes
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }

            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
        }
        # #AI countries will avoid taking new world colonies (e.g. from Argentina) when not proper
        # OR = {
            # THIS = { ai = no }
            # THIS = {
                # capital_scope = {
                    # NOT = {
                        # continent = europe
                        # continent = asia
                        # continent = africa
                    # }
                # }
            # }
            # any_owned_province = {
                # NOT = {
                    # continent = north_america
                    # continent = south_america
                # }
            # }
            # any_owned_province = { NOT = { any_core = { has_country_flag = new_world_nation } } }
            # any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
            # any_owned_province = { terrain = new_world_small_island }
            # any_owned_province = { terrain = new_world_arctic }
            # any_owned_province = {
                # OR = {
                    # is_core = CUB
                    # is_core = HAI
                    # is_core = DOM
                    # is_core = CAN
                # }
            # }

        # }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                port = yes
                any_neighbor_province = { owner = { tag = THIS } }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_COLONIAL_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Gain control of State
acquire_state = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            war_with = THIS
        }
        any_state = {
            is_colonial = no
            NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        }
		is_substate = no
		OR = {
			THIS = { civilized = no }
			NOT = { year = 1860 }
		}
        OR = {
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            civilized = yes
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI anti military will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        #AI will not use this CB when duking it out over hegemony
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    culture_has_union_tag = yes
                    is_culture_group = THIS
                    cultural_union = { exists = no }
                    is_greater_power = yes
                    THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        #Countries can't take capitals or cores (except cores in SW before 1834)
        NOT = {
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
                NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = sw_set
						NOT = { year = 1834 }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
					}
				}
			}
            any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        }

        #AI treats colonial states with only civilized cores as regular states
        OR = {
            is_colonial = no
            AND = {
                is_colonial = yes
                THIS = { ai = yes }
                any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = yes } }
                NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = no } } }
            }
        }

        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			#Player in MP can take anything they want from other players
			AND = {
				owner = { ai = no }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}

            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}

            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }

            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        is_greater_power = yes
                        is_secondary_power = yes
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }

            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
			#Player can take any state neighboring their vassal
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								substate_of = THIS
								vassal_of = THIS
							}
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
        }

        #AI will not grab cores of allies/spherelings
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        OR = {
                            alliance_with = THIS
                            in_sphere = THIS
                            vassal_of = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #pro-military AI will not grab cores of non-existing, non-union countries
        #unless they own some cores or it's part of their culture group and they're pro-military
        #jingoistic countries will also take states with existing cores that they also own some of
        #fascist & communist countries are exempt from this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = pro_military }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        is_cultural_union = no
                        exists = no
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            is_culture_group = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            AND = {
                                exists = no
                                is_cultural_union = no
                                is_culture_group = THIS
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

acquire_state_mid = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		THIS = { civilized = yes }
		civilized = yes
		year = 1860
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        any_state = {
            is_colonial = no
            NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI anti military will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        #AI will not use this CB when duking it out over hegemony
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    culture_has_union_tag = yes
                    is_culture_group = THIS
                    cultural_union = { exists = no }
                    is_greater_power = yes
                    THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
                }
            }
        }
		NOT = { year = 1880 }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        #Countries can't take capitals or cores
        NOT = {
            any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
            any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        }

        #AI treats colonial states with only civilized cores as regular states
        OR = {
            is_colonial = no
            AND = {
                is_colonial = yes
                THIS = { ai = yes }
                any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = yes } }
                NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = no } } }
            }
        }

        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			#Player in MP can take anything they want from other players
			AND = {
				owner = { ai = no }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}

            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}

            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }

            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        is_greater_power = yes
                        is_secondary_power = yes
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }

            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
			#Player can take any state neighboring their vassal
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								substate_of = THIS
								vassal_of = THIS
							}
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
        }

        #AI will not grab cores of allies/spherelings
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        OR = {
                            alliance_with = THIS
                            in_sphere = THIS
                            vassal_of = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #pro-military AI will not grab cores of non-existing, non-union countries
        #unless they own some cores or it's part of their culture group and they're pro-military
        #jingoistic countries will also take states with existing cores that they also own some of
        #fascist & communist countries are exempt from this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = pro_military }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        is_cultural_union = no
                        exists = no
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            is_culture_group = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            AND = {
                                exists = no
                                is_cultural_union = no
                                is_culture_group = THIS
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25

		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}

# Gain control of State
acquire_state_late = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 1.1
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.45
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		THIS = { civilized = yes }
		civilized = yes
		year = 1880
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        any_state = {
            is_colonial = no
            NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI anti military will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        #AI will not use this CB when duking it out over hegemony
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    culture_has_union_tag = yes
                    is_culture_group = THIS
                    cultural_union = { exists = no }
                    is_greater_power = yes
                    THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
                }
            }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        #Countries can't take capitals or cores
        NOT = {
            any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
            any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        }

        #AI treats colonial states with only civilized cores as regular states
        OR = {
            is_colonial = no
            AND = {
                is_colonial = yes
                THIS = { ai = yes }
                any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = yes } }
                NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = no } } }
            }
        }

        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			#Player in MP can take anything they want from other players
			AND = {
				owner = { ai = no }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}

            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }

            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }

            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        is_greater_power = yes
                        is_secondary_power = yes
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }

            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
			#Player can take any state neighboring their vassal
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								substate_of = THIS
								vassal_of = THIS
							}
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
        }

        #AI will not grab cores of allies/spherelings
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        OR = {
                            alliance_with = THIS
                            in_sphere = THIS
                            vassal_of = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #pro-military AI will not grab cores of non-existing, non-union countries
        #unless they own some cores or it's part of their culture group and they're pro-military
        #jingoistic countries will also take states with existing cores that they also own some of
        #fascist & communist countries are exempt from this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = pro_military }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        is_cultural_union = no
                        exists = no
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            is_culture_group = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            AND = {
                                exists = no
                                is_cultural_union = no
                                is_culture_group = THIS
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Chinese Reunification
china_acquire_state = {
    sprite_index = 22
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 84

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    always = yes

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            is_culture_group = east_asian
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                war_policy = pacifism
            }
        }
		any_owned_province = {
			any_neighbor_province = {
				owner = { tag = THIS }
			}
		}
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                is_core = CHI
            }
            is_culture_group = east_asian
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_global_flag = warlord_era_has_begun }
            owns = 1616
            NOT = { is_culture_group = east_asian }
            AND = {
                tag = CHI
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = neutral_faction } }
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction } }
            }
            AND = {
                tag = TPG
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = neutral_faction } }
            }
            AND = {
                tag = KMT
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = neutral_faction } }
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = beiyang_faction } }
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = communist_faction } }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { tag = TPG }
                OR = {
                    has_country_flag = beiyang_faction
                    has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction
                    has_country_flag = communist_faction
                    tag = KMT
                    THIS = { NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = beiyang_faction has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction has_country_flag = communist_faction tag = CHI tag = KMT } } } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { tag = KMT }
                OR = {
                    has_country_flag = beiyang_faction
                    tag = CHI
                    THIS = { NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = beiyang_faction tag = CHI tag = TPG } } } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { has_country_flag = beiyang_faction }
                OR = {
                    has_country_flag = beiyang_faction
                    THIS = { NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = beiyang_faction tag = CHI tag = TPG } } } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction }
                OR = {
                    has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction
                    THIS = { NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction tag = TPG tag = KMT } } } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { has_country_flag = communist_faction }
                OR = {
                    has_country_flag = communist_faction
                    THIS = { NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = communist_faction tag = TPG tag = CHI } } } }
                }
            }
        }
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1834 }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                    is_core = CHI
                    owner = { civilized = yes }
                }
                year = 1900
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                    is_core = CHI
                }
                THIS = { ai = no }
            }
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                is_core = CHI
                owner = { civilized = no }
            }
            any_owned_province = {
                owner = { is_culture_group = east_asian }
                NOT = { is_core = CHI }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CHINA_REUNIFICATION

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.10
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

sahel_jihad_cb = {
    sprite_index = 29
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 1.25

    badboy_factor = 2
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    can_use = {
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                province_id = 1786
                province_id = 1789
                province_id = 3787
                province_id = 3830
                province_id = 1794
                province_id = 3770
                province_id = 1800
                province_id = 1804
                province_id = 1808
                province_id = 1878
                province_id = 3831
                province_id = 1880
                province_id = 3778
                province_id = 3780
            }
        }
        THIS = {
            civilized = no
            OR = {
                government = theocracy
                government = absolute_monarchy
            }
            primary_culture = fulbe
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
        }
        civilized = no
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_flag = sunni_country }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
            AND = { owner = { war_with = THIS } THIS = { ai = no } }
        }
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS } }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_SAHEL_JIHAD_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Demand Concession
demand_concession_casus_belli = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    construction_speed = 1.2
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                OR = {
                    THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                    THIS = { ai = no }
                }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        THIS = {
            civilized = yes
            NOT = { nationalism_n_imperialism = 1 }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = berlin_conference }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { civilized = yes ai = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                civilization_progress = 0.6
                has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
            }
            AND = {
                tag = KOR
                THIS = { primary_culture = japanese }
            }
        }
        civilized = no
        number_of_states = 2
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { war_policy = jingoism NOT = { government = democracy } }
            NOT = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        capital_scope = { continent = south_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = north_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = no }

        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			#Player can take any state neighboring their vassal
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								substate_of = THIS
								vassal_of = THIS
							}
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                owner = { war_with = THIS }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        alliance_with = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering
        OR = {
			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
            continent = africa
            continent = central_africa
            continent = west_africa
            continent = east_africa
            continent = south_africa

            NOT = { total_pops = 500000 }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_logistics = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        raider_group_doctrine = 1
                        iron_steamers = 1
                    }
                }
            }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 2000000 }
                THIS = { machine_guns = 1 }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_directionism = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        steam_turbine_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 3000000 }
                THIS = {
                    bolt_action_rifles = 1
                    army_risk_management = 1
                }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_integration = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        oil_driven_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                total_pops = 3000000
                THIS = {
                    modern_divisional_structure = 1
                    army_nco_training = 1
                }
            }
        } ###End of Non-African Restrictions

    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONCESSION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Bad Boy
rude_boy = {
    sprite_index = 28
    is_triggered_only = no
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 2
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 1.5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = yes

    can_use = {
        badboy = 1
        is_disarmed = no
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }

        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
				relation = { who = THIS value = 1 }
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
			AND = {
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
				relation = { who = THIS value = 1 }
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
			AND = {
				government = radical_republic
				THIS = { government = radical_republic }
				relation = { who = THIS value = 1 }
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
		}
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes
    po_disarmament = yes
    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = WAR_RUDEBOI_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Conquest
conquest = {
    sprite_index = 2
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                any_state = {
                    is_colonial = no
                    NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        government = proletarian_dictatorship
                        government = fascist_dictatorship
                    }

                }
                NOT = { number_of_states = 4 }
            }
            AND = {
                tag = SWI
                NOT = { number_of_states = 4 }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI anti-military will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI will not use this when fighting for hegemony
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                    any_greater_power = {
                        war_with = THIS
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        is_culture_group = THIS
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                    }
                    THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        is_greater_power = yes
                        is_secondary_power = yes
                    }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI will not grab cores of allies/spherelings
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        OR = {
                            alliance_with = THIS
                            in_sphere = THIS
                            vassal_of = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #pro-military AI will not grab cores of non-existing, non-union countries
        #unless they own some cores or it's part of their culture group
        #jingoistic will also grab existing cores that they already own some of
        #fascist & communist countries are exempt from this
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = pro_military }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        is_cultural_union = no
                        exists = no
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            is_culture_group = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            AND = {
                                exists = no
                                is_cultural_union = no
                                is_culture_group = THIS
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				THIS = { ai = no }
				NOT = { total_pops = 400000 }
				NOT = { number_of_states = 3 }
			}
		}
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                has_country_modifier = disable_conquest_cb
            }
        }
    }

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 5
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONQUEST_NAME
}

# Berlin Conference
annex_africa = {
    sprite_index = 22
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 1.5

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 2

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 0

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = yes

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            has_global_flag = berlin_conference
			colonial_nation = yes
            nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
            capital_scope = { continent = europe }
            slavery = no_slavery
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality }
            civilized = yes
            NOT = { tag = RUS }
            NOT = { tag = TUR }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        number_of_states = 2
        civilized = no
        OR = {
            capital_scope = { continent = africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = central_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = west_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects }
            }
        }
        #Claimed colonial regions can't be conquered with this CB
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = colonial_railroading_disabled
			NOT = {
				THIS = { tag = POR ai = yes }
			}
		}
        NOT = { has_country_flag = cfs_owner }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = {
            tag = MOR
            tag = ALD
            tag = TRI
            tag = CYR
            tag = LIB
            tag = ETH
            tag = MAD
            tag = EGY
            has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
        }
        ai = yes
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = no }
        #NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONCESSION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

                            region = EGY_1762
                            region = EGY_1771
                        }
                    }
                }

                    OR = {
                        region = EGY_1745
                        region = EGY_1758
                        region = EGY_1762
                        region = EGY_1771
                        region = EGY_1755
                    }
                }
            }
            #Sudan
            AND = {

                        OR = {
                            region = EGY_1834
                            region = EGY_1827
                            region = EGY_1838
                            region = ENG_1844
                            #region = EGY_1842
                        }
                    }
                }

                        region = EGY_1834

                        region = EGY_1838
                        region = ENG_1844
                        #region = EGY_1842
                    }
                }
            }
            #Ethiopia
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    NOT = { tag = TUR }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        OR = {
                            region = ETH_1853
                            region = ETH_1852
                            region = ETH_1859
							region = ETH_1867
							region = ETH_3591
                        }
                    }
                }
                any_owned_province = {
                    OR = {

						region = ETH_1867

                        }

# Establish Protectorate
establish_protectorate_casus_belli = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {

		THIS = {
            civilized = yes
			NOT = {
				nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
				has_global_flag = berlin_conference
				has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
			}
        }
		OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
		civilized = no
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
            }
            AND = {
                tag = KOR
                THIS = { tag = JAP }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }

        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { war_policy = jingoism NOT = { government = democracy } }
            NOT = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        capital_scope = { continent = south_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = north_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering
        OR = {
			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
            capital_scope = { continent = africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = west_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = central_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }

            NOT = { total_pops = 500000 }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_logistics = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        raider_group_doctrine = 1
                        iron_steamers = 1
                    }
                }
            }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 2000000 }
                THIS = { machine_guns = 1 }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_directionism = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        steam_turbine_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 3000000 }
                THIS = {
                    bolt_action_rifles = 1
                    army_risk_management = 1
                }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_integration = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        oil_driven_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                total_pops = 3000000
                THIS = {
                    modern_divisional_structure = 1
                    army_nco_training = 1
                }
            }
        } ###End of Non-African Restrictions

        NOT = {
			is_our_vassal = THIS
			has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
			number_of_states = 2
		}
    }

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_PROTECTORATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
    on_po_accepted = { tech_school = unciv_tech_school }
}

    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0

    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

        ai = no

        number_of_states = 2 # annex if you want their last state
        is_vassal = no
        THIS = { civilized = yes }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_NEGOTIATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.00
        }
    }
}

end_jihad = {
    sprite_index = 21
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 8
    crisis = no

    can_use = {
        THIS = { ai = no has_country_flag = i_am_segou has_global_flag = no_more_fula_jihad is_vassal = no }
        total_pops = 20000
		religion = sunni
		OR = {
			primary_culture = fulbe
			primary_culture = gur
			primary_culture = mande
		}
		NOT = { tag = SOK }
		OR = {
			tag = JAL
			tag = TOO
			tag = BTE
			tag = BDU
			tag = GNE
			tag = NIG
		}
		is_vassal = no
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            war_with = THIS
        }
        NOT = { total_pops = 800000 }
    }

    badboy_factor = 1.2
    prestige_factor = 5
    peace_cost_factor = 80
    penalty_factor = 2

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    war_name = END_JIHAD_WAR_NAME
	
    po_remove_prestige = yes
    po_disarmament = yes
    po_reparations = yes

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					tag = JAL
				}
			}
			owner = {
				any_owned = {
					limit = {
						is_core = GBU
					}
					secede_province = THIS
					secede_province = GBU
				}
				any_owned = {
					limit = {
						province_id = 3778
					}
					secede_province = THIS
					secede_province = GBU
					add_core = GBU
				}
				any_owned = {
					limit = {
						is_core = MLI
					}
					secede_province = THIS
					secede_province = MLI
				}
				any_owned = {
					limit = {
						is_core = SEG
					}
					secede_province = THIS
					secede_province = SEG
				}
				any_owned = {
					limit = {
						is_core = BTE
					}
					secede_province = THIS
					secede_province = BTE
				}
				government = absolute_monarchy
			}
		}
		random_owned = {

				ENG = {
					any_owned = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								continent = north_america
								continent = south_america
							}
						}
						remove_core = ENG
						secede_province = THIS
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Make Puppet
make_puppet = {
    sprite_index = 18
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 2.0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		total_pops = 400000
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            war_with = THIS
            any_neighbor_country = {
                OR = {
                    vassal_of = THIS
                    substate_of = THIS
                    in_sphere = THIS
                }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
            OR = {
				AND = {
					total_pops = 5000000
					NOT = { has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp }
				}
				AND = {
					total_pops = 2000000
					has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
				}
			}
        }
        is_vassal = no
        is_greater_power = no
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
		ai = yes
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope

    po_make_puppet = yes

    war_name = WAR_PUPPET_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        country_event = 19370
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Become Independent
become_independent = {
    sprite_index = 10
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    always = yes

    badboy_factor = 1
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 108

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            THIS = { substate_of = FROM }
        }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        NOT = { AND = { tag = EGY ai = yes } }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        OR = {
            FROM = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
            war_with = THIS
        }
    }

    po_release_puppet = yes
    po_add_to_sphere = yes

    war_name = WAR_INDEPENDENCE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
        add_war_goal = {
            casus_belli = make_puppet
        }
        leave_alliance = FROM
        release_vassal = THIS
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Revert from Communist Government
uninstall_communist_gov_cb = {
    sprite_index = 13
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    # Is automatically added to countries that intervened at while install_communist_gov_cb
    # so they can revert those countries government.
    constructing_cb = no

    badboy_factor = 0.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        government = proletarian_dictatorship
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = {
                    has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                }
            }
        }
        THIS = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } }
    }

    po_uninstall_communist_gov_type = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

    sprite_index = 19
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 1.5
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 50
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        has_global_flag = great_wars_enabled
        THIS = {
            is_greater_power = yes
            OR = {
                government = hms_government
                government = constitutional_empire
                government = democracy
            }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war }
        }
        civilized = yes
        OR = {
            government = proletarian_dictatorship
            government = fascist_dictatorship
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = in_great_war
                    has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes

    war_name = DEMOCRACY_WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.05
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        THIS = {
            set_country_flag = friendly_democracy

                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        government = proletarian_dictatorship
                        government = fascist_dictatorship

                }

            }
        }
        country_event = 96085

    }

# Gain control of Substate region
acquire_substate_region = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = { ai = no }
        num_of_substates = 1 # if has any substate
        any_substate = {
            OR = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = { tag = THIS }
					}
				}
                AND = {
                    THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
            number_of_states = 1
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                is_colonial = no
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_substate_regions = {
        is_colonial = no
        #owner = { NOT = { in_sphere = THIS } }
        any_owned_province = {
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
            is_colonial = no
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_SUBSTATE_REGION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Gain control of Substate Core region
acquire_substate_core_region = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no
    always = yes

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = { ai = no }
        num_of_substates = 1 # if has any substate
        any_substate = {
            any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
            #NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
            OR = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                AND = {
                    THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = { tag = THIS }
					}
				}
            }
            NOT = { in_sphere = THIS }
            number_of_states = 1
        }
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1834 }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_substate_regions = {
        any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
        #NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            AND = {
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
        }
        owner = { NOT = { in_sphere = THIS } }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}
