# Dismantle fortifications (forts + naval bases)
dismantle_forts = {
    sprite_index = 16
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 1
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1


    can_use = {
        THIS = { civilized = yes }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state
    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                has_building = fort
                has_building = naval_base
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
            }
        }
    }

    po_destroy_forts = yes
    po_destroy_naval_bases = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }


	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

#Placeholder for acquire state-by-event
acquire_any_state = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    constructing_cb = no
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 0
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

	always = no

    can_use = {
        is_vassal = no
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        #Countries can't take capitals
        NOT = {
            any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        }

        #AI treats colonial states with only civilized cores as regular states
        OR = {
            is_colonial = no
            AND = {
                is_colonial = yes
                THIS = { ai = yes }
                any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = yes } }
                NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = no } } }
            }
        }

        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			#Player in MP can take anything they want from other players
			AND = {
				owner = { ai = no }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}

            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}

            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }

            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        is_greater_power = yes
                        is_secondary_power = yes
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }

            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    civilized = no
                    is_culture_group = east_asian
                    OR = {
                        owns = 1481
                        owns = 1496
                        owns = 1498
                        owns = 1538
						owns = 3364
                        owns = 1566
                        owns = 1569
                        owns = 1606
                        owns = 2632
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    civilized = yes
                    NOT = { is_culture_group = east_asian }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
            owner = { country_event = 1316089 }
        }
    }
}

spanish_reconquista = {
    sprite_index = 2
    is_triggered_only = no
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    always = yes

    can_use = {
		THIS = {
			has_global_flag = reconquista
			OR = {
				tag = SPA
				tag = SPC
				tag = IBR
			}
			primary_culture = spanish
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_american_war }

			tag = PTG
			tag = PBC
			tag = LPL
			tag = ENT
			tag = CRT
			tag = DOM
		}
        OR = {
            THIS = {
  			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        THIS = {
            OR = {
                is_secondary_power = yes
                is_greater_power = yes
            }
            OR = {
                government = absolute_monarchy
                government = prussian_constitutionalism
                government = hms_government
                government = absolute_empire
                government = semi_constitutional_empire
                government = constitutional_empire
            }
            NOT = { revolution_n_counterrevolution = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }
    }

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_RECONQUISTA_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
		THIS = {
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp }
					}
				}
				owner = {
					badboy = 5
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
					}
				}
				owner = {
					badboy = 11
				}
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						tag = DOM
						tag = TBS
						tag = OAX
						tag = TRS
						tag = YUC
						tag = LOS
						tag = CHP
						tag = GUA
						tag = ELS
						tag = HON
						tag = NIC
						tag = PNM
						tag = URU
						tag = PRG
						tag = ENT
						tag = CRT
						tag = TEX
						tag = RGR
						tag = COS
					}
				}
			}
			THIS = {
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = { has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp }
						}
					}
					owner = {
						badboy = -4
					}
				}
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
						}
					}
					owner = {
						badboy = -6
					}
				}
			}
		}
		USA = { casus_belli = { target = THIS type = humiliate months = 120 } casus_belli = { target = THIS type = cut_down_to_size months = 120 } }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_culture_group = latin_american_cultures
				exists = yes
			}
			casus_belli = { target = THIS type = humiliate months = 120 }
			casus_belli = { target = THIS type = liberate_country months = 120 }
			relation = { who = THIS value = -400 }
			leave_alliance = THIS
		}
    }
    on_po_accepted = {
		USA = { casus_belli = { target = THIS type = free_peoples months = 12 } }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_culture_group = latin_american_cultures
				exists = yes
				NOT = { primary_culture = brazilian }
			}
			casus_belli = { target = THIS type = free_peoples months = 12 }
		}
	}
}

    can_use = {
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 0
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONQUEST_ANY_NAME

    on_add = {
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        THIS = {
            random_owned = {
                limit = { is_core = TRN TRN = { exists = no has_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest } }
                THIS = { release_vassal = TRN }
                TRN = { clr_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest civilized = no annex_to = THIS }
                TRN = { civilized = yes }
            }
            random_owned = {
                limit = { is_core = ORA ORA = { exists = no has_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest } }
                THIS = { release_vassal = ORA }
                ORA = { clr_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest civilized = no annex_to = THIS }
                ORA = { civilized = yes }
            }
            random_owned = {
                limit = { is_core = NAL NAL = { exists = no has_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest } }
                THIS = { release_vassal = NAL }
                NAL = { clr_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest civilized = no annex_to = THIS }
                NAL = { civilized = yes }
            }
        }
    }

    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

end_radicals = {
    sprite_index = 37
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 5
    prestige_factor = 4
    peace_cost_factor = 75
    penalty_factor = 1
	always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		government = radical_republic
		is_vassal = no
        civilized = yes
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
			AND = {
				has_country_modifier = francia_utopia
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
		THIS = {
			NOT = {
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				government = democracy
				government = radical_republic
				ruling_party_ideology = radical
			}
		}
    }

	po_add_to_sphere = yes
	po_remove_prestige = yes

    war_name = WAR_END_RADICALS_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.05
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		set_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
		THIS = {
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = conservative
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
						}
						ruling_party_ideology = conservative
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = liberal
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
						}
						ruling_party_ideology = liberal
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
						}
						ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = socialist
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {

guillotine_cb = {
    sprite_index = 36
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 5
    prestige_factor = 4
    peace_cost_factor = 75
    penalty_factor = 1
	always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		THIS = { government = radical_republic }
		is_vassal = no
        civilized = yes
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
		NOT = {
			government = democracy
			government = radical_republic
		}
    }

	po_remove_prestige = yes

    war_name = WAR_GUILLOTINE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.05
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		THIS = { set_country_flag = sister_republic_boss }
		country_event = 191337
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        THIS = {
            random_list = {
                20 = { add_country_modifier = { name = claimed_africa duration = 365 } }
                20 = { add_country_modifier = { name = claimed_africa duration = 730 } }
                20 = { add_country_modifier = { name = claimed_africa duration = 1095 } }
                20 = { add_country_modifier = { name = claimed_africa duration = 1460 } }
                20 = { add_country_modifier = { name = claimed_africa duration = 1825 } }
            }
        }
    }
}

# War Reparations
war_reparations = {
    sprite_index = 27
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0.2
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            civilized = yes
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }
        war_with = THIS
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
            has_country_modifier = no_more_war
            has_country_flag = in_great_war
        }
    }

    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME_REPARATIONS

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    tag = HAI
                    FRA = { is_greater_power = yes }
                    NOT = { has_country_flag = agreed_to_pay_debt }
                }
            }
            owner = {
                country_event = 45108
            }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    tag = MEX
                    has_country_flag = pay_1st_pastry_war
                }
            }
            owner = {
                country_event = 45108
            }
        }
    }
}

                    }
                }
            }
            #Somalia
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = {
                        OR = {
                            region = SOM_1868
                            region = SOM_1872
							region = SOM_1871
                        }
                    }
                }
                any_owned_province = {
                    OR = {
                        region = SOM_1868
                        region = SOM_1872
						region = SOM_1871
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        THIS = {
            nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
            capital_scope = { continent = europe }
            NOT = { tag = RUS }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = cfs_master }
            has_global_flag = berlin_conference
        }

        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects }
            }
        }
        NOT = { in_sphere = THIS }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_flag = post_colonial_country }
        NOT = { number_of_states = 2 }
        ai = yes
    }

    po_annex = yes

#Take Capital
take_capital = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 3
    prestige_factor = 10
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 36

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        number_of_states = 2 # annex if you want their last state
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = {
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
        }
        any_owned_province = {
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
            is_colonial = no
        }
        is_vassal = no
        OR = {
            AND = {
                civilized = yes
                THIS = {
                    civilized = yes
                }
            }
            AND = {
                civilized = no
                THIS = {
                    civilized = no
                }
            }
        }
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = in_great_war
                has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
            }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1834 }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
            }
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        is_colonial = no
        any_owned_province = {
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
            is_colonial = no
        }
        any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                owner = { war_with = THIS }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        alliance_with = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering
        OR = {
			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
            continent = africa
            continent = central_africa
            continent = west_africa
            continent = east_africa
            continent = south_africa

            NOT = { total_pops = 500000 }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_logistics = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        raider_group_doctrine = 1
                        iron_steamers = 1
                    }
                }
            }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 2000000 }
                THIS = { machine_guns = 1 }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_directionism = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        steam_turbine_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 3000000 }
                THIS = {
                    bolt_action_rifles = 1
                    army_risk_management = 1
                }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_integration = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        oil_driven_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                total_pops = 3000000
                THIS = {
                    modern_divisional_structure = 1
                    army_nco_training = 1
                }
            }
        } ###End of Non-African Restrictions

    }


    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONCESSION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}


demand_concession_capital_early = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 1

    badboy_factor = 2.3
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 60

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
			civilized = yes
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = in_great_war
                has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
				has_global_flag = berlin_conference
				nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
            }
        }
        any_owned_province = {
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
            is_colonial = no
        }
        number_of_states = 2 # annex if you want their last state
        OR = {
            AND = {
                OR = {
                    THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                    THIS = { ai = no }
                }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        civilized = no
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = no }
        any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}

                THIS = { ai = no }

            }

                NOT = {

                        exists = yes
                        alliance_with = THIS

                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }

			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
            continent = africa
            continent = central_africa
            continent = west_africa

            continent = south_africa

    sprite_index = 6

    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2

    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        num_of_substates = 1 # if has any substate

            number_of_states = 1
            any_owned_province = {
                is_core = THIS
                is_colonial = no
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_substate_regions = {
        is_colonial = no
        owner = { NOT = { in_sphere = THIS } }
        any_owned_province = {
            is_core = THIS
            is_colonial = no
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {

            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Liberate puppet
liberate_puppet = {
    sprite_index = 18
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.3

    badboy_factor = 2.8
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 0

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1


    can_use = {
        OR = {
            THIS = {
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        number_of_states = 2
        THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality
			has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
        THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality } }
		ai = yes
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        FROM = { exists = no }
        OR = {
            is_releasable_vassal = FROM
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            FROM = { NOT = { any_core = { is_core = THIS } } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        NOT = {
            tag = FROM
            FROM = { tag = THIS }
            FROM = { tag = MTC }
            this_culture_union = FROM
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = ETH }
                NOT = { exists = ETH }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = BOL }
                exists = PBC
            }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    OR = {
						any_owned_province = {
							any_neighbor_province = {
								owner = { tag = THIS }
							}
						}
                        controlled_by = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                FROM = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								in_sphere = THIS
								alliance_with = THIS
								tag = THIS
							}
						}
                    }
                    controlled_by = THIS
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    continent = europe
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    OR = {
                        continent = north_america
                        continent = south_america
                    }
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    OR = {
                        continent = north_america
                        continent = south_america
                    }
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = asia } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    continent = asia
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                FROM = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
        }
        FROM = {
            OR = {
                is_cultural_union = no
                involved_in_crisis = yes
            }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            FROM = { civilized = yes }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state
    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            is_core = FROM
        }
    }
    all_allowed_states = yes
    po_transfer_provinces = yes

    war_name = WAR_LIBERATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                exists = no
                has_country_flag = existing_country
            }
            clr_country_flag = existing_country
        }
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                exists = no
                has_country_flag = vassal_nation_cb
            }
            clr_country_flag = vassal_nation_cb
        }
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        country_event = 2651    # Territorial Loss event
        THIS = { country_event = 19369 } # Starts puppeting event chain
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

    peace_cost_factor = 1

    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2

    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
        civilized = no

			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS

        OR = {
            war_with = THIS

    }

    po_annex = yes

demand_concession_casus_belli_no_infamy = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
	constructing_cb = no
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                OR = {
                    THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                    THIS = { ai = no }
                }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        civilized = no
        number_of_states = 2
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = no }

        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			#Player can take any state neighboring their vassal
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								substate_of = THIS
								vassal_of = THIS
							}
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                owner = { war_with = THIS }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }

    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONCESSION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }


	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}


# Cut Down to size
abolish_sound_dues_cb = {
    sprite_index = 43
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 1.3
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 25
    penalty_factor = 1
    constructing_cb = no
    crisis = no

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    po_disarmament = yes
    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = ABOLISH_SOUND_DUES_CB_WAR_NAME

    can_use = {
    }

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        372 = { trade_goods = grain remove_province_modifier = sound_dues_toll }
        clr_global_flag = sound_dues_resisted #No longer resisting
        set_global_flag = sound_dues_abolished #Have to abolish
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}
